REL-REF    (M,,M.Barbagallo+,J,EPJ/A,49,156,2013)                 2321000100070 
           Evaluated neutron flux is described.                   2321000100071 
           (M,,G.Lorusso+,J,NIM/A,532,622,2004)                   2321000100072 
           Method of time-of-flight to energy calibration,        2321000100073 
            based on the analysis of 197Au resonances.            2321000100074

           technique.                                             2321000100077

           Details of digital data acquisition system.            2321000100079 
FACILITY   (SYNCY,2ZZZCER) n TOF facility at CERN.                2321000100080 
           High-performance digital data acquisition system,      2321000100081 
           based on 8-bit flash analog-to-digital converter (FADC)2321000100082 
           units operating at a sampling rate of 500 MHz.         2321000100083 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL)   Neutrons are produced by an intense pulsed   2321000100084 
           beam of 20 GeV/c protons impinging on a massive        2321000100085 
           cylindrical Pb target. Repetition rate in multiples of 2321000100086 
           1.2 s and a proton pulse width of 7 ns. 300 neutrons   2321000100087 
           are produced per proton, resulting in a total of 2E+15 2321000100088 
           neutrons per pulse. The neutron beam is shaped by      2321000100089 
           collimators at 137 and 178 m from spallation target.   2321000100090 
INC-SPECT  Neutron spectrum spans the energy range from thermal   2321000100091 
           to several GeV.                                        2321000100092 
           With the second collimator in capture mode, the flux   2321000100093 
           of neutrons below 400 keV, integrated over the nearly  2321000100094 
           Gaussian beam profile at the sample position, amounts  2321000100095 
           to 2.2E+5 neutrons per pulse.                          2321000100096 
SAMPLE      58Ni sample of 2.069 g mass, 19.91 mm diameter,       2321000100097 
           0.72 mm (6.9E-3 at./barn) thickness, 99.5% enrichment. 2321000100098 
           Contained only 0.48% of 60Ni, 0.01% of 61Ni and        2321000100099 
           0.005% of both 62Ni and 64Ni.                          2321000100100 
           (28-NI-58,ENR=0.995)                                   2321000100101 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) Two C6D6 liquid scintillation detectors were    2321000100102 
           mounted 8.2 cm upstream of the sample and at a distance2321000100103 
           of 6.8 cm from the center of the neutron beam line.    2321000100104 
           The energy calibration of the C6D6 detectors was       2321000100105 
           performed with 137Cs, 88Y, Am/Be calibration sources,  2321000100106 
           which were also used to verify the stability of the    2321000100107 
           detector response during the 32 days of experiment.    2321000100108 
           The energy resolution of the two C6D6 detectors was    2321000100109 
           assessed from these calibration data.                  2321000100110 
           (SI) The neutron flux was monitored by SiMon - a       2321000100111 
           silicon-based neutron beam monitor based on the        2321000100112 
           6Li(n,t)alpha reaction.                                2321000100113 
METHOD     (TOF) 185 m.                                           2321000100114 
            Pulse height weighting technique.                     2321000100115 
           The detector response to a gamma ray of energy was     2321000100116 
           obtained by detailed GEANT4 simulation taking into     2321000100117 
           account the intrinsic and geometrical efficiency for   2321000100118 
           detecting gamma rays and secondary effects - absorption2321000100119 
           of gamma rays in the sample and the detection of       2321000100120 
           photons scattered by the nearby components.            2321000100121 
ANALYSIS   Simulated monochromatic spectra were folded with the   2321000100122 
           experimentally determined energy resolution of the two 2321000100123 
           C6D6 detectors. The cutoff threshold of 200 keV applied2321000100124 
           during offline analysis. The resulting spectra were    2321000100125 
           used to calculate the weighting function, assumed to be2321000100126 
           a polynomial of fourth degree.                         2321000100127 
           The absolute yield normalization factor was evaluated  2321000100128 
           by means of the saturated resonance technique, applied 2321000100129 
           to the 4.9 eV resonance of 197Au.                      2321000100130 
CORRECTION For backgrounds: from an empty sample holder,          2321000100131 
           the ambient background, the background from neutrons   2321000100132 
           scattered of the sample.                               2321000100133 
HISTORY    (20140120C) M.M.                                       2321000100134 
           Request for the data (Subents 004, 006) was sent       2321000100135 
           06.02.2014 to authors P.Zugec and R.Reifarth.          2321000100136 
           (20140207R) Data were received from P.Zugec 2 Feb.2014.2321000100137

REACTION   (28-NI-58(N,G),,WID)                                   2321000200003 
            Gamma widths for negative resonances.                 2321000200004 
ASSUMED    (ASSUM,28-NI-58(N,EL),,WID)    Elastic width           2321000200005 
ANALYSIS   The experimental data were fitted by a multilevel      2321000200006 
           R-matrix code SAMMY, which accounts for the resolution 2321000200007 
           function of the neutron beam, Doppler broadening of    2321000200008 
           capture resonances, multiple scattering and            2321000200009 
           self-shielding effects. The reasonable fit for energies2321000200010 
           up to 10 keV was obtained by considering two resonances2321000200011 
           with negative energy. The energy and neutron width of  2321000200012 
           the two resonances were fixed at the value adopted from2321000200013 
           the ENDF/B-VII.1,while the capture width was left free.2321000200014

           to the neutron energy of 25.3 meV.                     2321000300007
